border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>麦当劳被湘菜“赶跑了”。<br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>黄兴路步行街是长沙最繁华的地方，永远人头攒动，永远灯光闪烁。这条全长不足1000米的商业街位于长沙商业的心脏地段，几乎每个来长沙的游客都会来这里打卡，在大大小小的美食店铺门口排起长队。其中，最能汇聚流量的“铺王”位置当然位于步行街的入口，就在近代民主革命家黄兴的铜像旁边，基本承接了所有进入步行街的人流。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>在长达十五年的时间里，这个位置一直属于麦当劳。这很好理解，口味受众广泛、价格适中的西式快餐店已经是中国所有商圈的标配，总能占到好位置。而今年夏天，黄兴路步行街的“铺王”却从洋快餐变成了本土湘菜——柠檬黄底色上印着黑色粗体字：“炊烟小炒黄牛肉”。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>八月的长沙热浪滚滚，但这无法阻挡人们对一口真正美味的小炒黄牛肉的渴求。自炊烟小炒黄牛肉黄兴铜像店7月31日试运营以来，从上午11点到晚上11点都有人在门口排队，12个小时不曾间断。炊烟小炒黄牛肉总裁谭艳透露，这个店每天取号2000多桌，翻台率达11次以上。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden center break-word><img data-ratio=\"0.748792270531401\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"828\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box; vertical-align: top; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/LrRuh3G4W5znch9tZfChic7micsaiaxeXhCDoh0PVwzwlPMicQapCHthDnTiawkPyc11uLOUhNAoh3UOPYN3OXEPFhw/640?wx_fmt=png\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">一道代表着传统湘菜的小炒黄牛肉，凭啥“赶跑”麦当劳？</strong></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p label=\"大标题\" style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden bold center break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;display: block;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;width: 265px !important;\"><em style=\"margin-top: 9px;margin-right: 10px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;width: 12px;display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;background-size: 100% 100%;height: 8px;background-image: url(\" https: no-repeat break-word></em><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;z-index: 10000;line-height: 1.65;max-width: 250px !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">为什么湘菜从前不够火？</span><em style=\"margin-top: 8px;margin-left: 10px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;width: 12px;display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;background-size: 100% 100%;height: 11px;background-image: url(\" https: no-repeat break-word></em></span></span></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>“铺王”位置的更换之所以让人惊讶，是因为湘菜以前缺乏一个让全国人民印象深刻的品牌——明明和川菜一样以辣著称，可为什么在湖南以外，湘菜的整体面目总显得模糊？</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>中国传统饮食文化有“八大菜系”的说法，指的是川菜、鲁菜、粤菜、闽菜、淮扬菜、浙菜、湘菜、徽菜。八大菜系究竟该怎么排序，没人能说得清：四川人喜欢把川菜排在第一位，山东人则认为鲁菜才是历史悠久的“宫廷正菜”。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>清代笔记汇编《清稗类钞》曾对晚清各地的饮食喜好做了归类：“北人嗜葱蒜，滇、黔、湘、蜀人嗜辛辣品，粤人嗜淡食，苏人嗜糖。”</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>《清稗类钞》没有具体地提出“菜系”的概念，但这成了后来“四大菜系”倡导者的理论依据。改革开放后，随着中国的饮食消费行业逐步复苏，有学者主张“四大菜系”的说法，主推鲁（华北）、粤（华南）、川（云桂湘鄂）、淮扬（华东）。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>到了20世纪九十年代，在各地烹饪协会的争执与推荐中，“八大菜系”菜渐渐成为全国通用的说法，在“四大菜系”的基础上添了浙、闽、湘、徽。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>发现了没有？哪怕被囊括进了八大菜系，湘菜的排位依然靠后，存在感不强。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>地方菜系进军全国市场，需要拥有标准化、品牌化的运作能力，这样才能保证口味的稳定性、打入更广的市场。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>同是以“辣”为主基调的菜系，川菜包含火锅、串串、麻辣烫等品类，这种食材+调味的搭配对厨师的要求较低，更容易标准化。而湘菜的主要烹饪技法为炒与蒸。湖南省湘菜产业促进协会会长肖志军认为，一个“炒”字，点出了湘菜的本质：左边是火右边是少，火候的多少要靠厨师来把控。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>这就意味着，湘菜对厨师技术、锅具与食材的要求都比较高，因此更难标准化，餐饮湘军们跨区域经营的挑战也更大。想要塑造出一个全国闻名的湘菜品牌，难上加难。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>如今，江浙菜已经跑出了外婆家、绿茶等全国连锁品牌，川菜也有眉州东坡和小龙坎等一众火锅连锁品牌，粤菜则有陶陶居、点都德、广州酒家等闻名在外。但要是让外地人想想有什么足以代表湖南的餐饮品牌，恐怕大多数人都难以迅速从脑海里捞出一个准确的名字。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>根据世界中餐业联合会、红餐网等联合发布的《2019中国餐饮品牌力白皮书》，“2019年度中国餐饮品牌力百强”名单中包含44个中式正餐品牌，从菜系来看，粤菜与江浙菜分别上榜11家和9家，依然领先；川菜、京帮菜紧随其后，分别有5家与4家上榜。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>对餐饮湘军来说，湘菜的品牌化经营，还有很长的路要走。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>《白皮书》这样总结中国餐饮品牌力的发展历程：在1990年之前，中国餐饮都以个体户经营为主，缺乏品牌意识；1990年~2000年则是“萌芽期”，正是洋快餐的涌入才刺激了行业发展，促使中国餐饮人逐步形成品牌意识。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>如今，炊烟小炒黄牛肉代替了洋快餐麦当劳、一跃成为长沙新“铺王”，颇有时代更迭之意味——餐饮湘军的品牌力，正在养成。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word> </p><p label=\"大标题\" style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden bold center break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;display: block;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;width: 265px !important;\"><em style=\"margin-top: 9px;margin-right: 10px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;width: 12px;display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;background-size: 100% 100%;height: 8px;background-image: url(\" https: no-repeat break-word></em><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;z-index: 10000;line-height: 1.65;max-width: 250px !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">一道小炒黄牛肉</span><em style=\"margin-top: 8px;margin-left: 10px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;width: 12px;display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;background-size: 100% 100%;height: 11px;background-image: url(\" https: no-repeat break-word></em></span></span></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden center break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;font-weight: bold;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">如</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;font-weight: bold;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">何扛起“湘军</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;font-weight: bold;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">”大旗？</span></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>从炊烟的外在表现来看，它具备了所谓“网红”的一切特征：热度极高、大排长龙，吃过一顿以后，朋友圈的九宫格就有了着落。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word> </p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>由于排号时间长，炊烟被赋予了“长沙三大排队王”的称号——和它并列的，是以还原老长沙情景为特色的超级文和友与“只在长沙才能喝到”的茶颜悦色。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word> </p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>去超级文和友打卡拍照、喝一杯清甜茶底上浮着奶油忌廉的茶颜悦色、尝一口炊烟小炒黄牛肉，位列年轻游客们来长沙的“To Do List”前三名。在社交平台的旅游攻略里，你总能找到这“<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">长沙美食三大天王</strong>”。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden center break-word><img data-ratio=\"0.7493975903614458\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"830\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box; vertical-align: top; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/LrRuh3G4W5znch9tZfChic7micsaiaxeXhCQezfMibbYcpvibPmicl57uRQicuJjdjTtWIOw0rnvH3AQzn0dQUNEyfMIA/640?wx_fmt=png\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>但炊烟跟其他网红餐饮店最大的不同之处，是它已经网红了足足22年。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>1998年，炊烟创始人戴宗在衡阳创办了“花明楼酒家”，主营湘菜宴请。后来迁至长沙，改名为“戴家村”湖南土菜馆，这便是炊烟小炒黄牛肉的前身。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>据谭艳介绍，戴家村一开始其实开在长沙郊区的新港镇，虽然地方偏僻，但一开业就成为最火爆的湘菜馆。顾客当时都是开车前来吃饭，停在路边的车子排成长龙，足足能排两公里，高峰期甚至需要交警在旁引导指挥。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>2009年，“戴家村”正式改名为“炊烟食代”；2016年，“炊烟食代”又改名为“炊烟时代”；2018年，炊烟时代再度进行品牌升级，正式把“小炒黄牛肉”放进了每家店的招牌上，成为炊烟的招牌菜。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>同年还有一件大事发生——炊烟小炒黄牛肉代表湘菜走进了联合国。2018年11月，美国纽约，炊烟小炒黄牛肉与剁椒鱼头、红烧肉等菜肴一起被呈上联合国总部宴会餐桌，受到联合国官员及各国嘉宾的高度关注与好评。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>更别提40余位一线明星的亲自“背书”：从2019年起，炊烟小炒黄牛肉相继出现在湖南卫视《天天向上》《向往的生活》《我家那小子》等节目里，成为2020湖南卫视春晚的指定湘菜——在这样阖家团聚的日子里，一道嫩滑多汁、香辣十足的小炒黄牛肉，代表了湖南人心中的家乡之味。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>从开在长沙郊区的小餐馆，到代表湘菜走进联合国的“湘菜领导者”，炊烟小炒黄牛肉在过去22年里的不少动作都值得餐饮同行借鉴。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>首先，这个湘菜品牌虽然“土生土长”，却相当崇尚创新、拥抱变化。22年里，炊烟两度更名，并不断进行品牌升级、修正品牌定位。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word> </p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>在2016年更名后，炊烟马上捕捉到了新的商业趋势：购物中心遍地开花，成为新的商业流量集中地。于是，炊烟也从路边逐渐开进长沙各大购物中心，据谭艳回忆，第一家开在购物中心的mall店在节假日就已经需要排队2小时才能吃上了。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>其次，炊烟在十几年前就开始有意地修炼企业“内功”——包括供应链、组织力、信息化能力等等。彼时，湘菜还处在同质化竞争的阶段，零散、非连锁的小馆子是市场主流。但当时的炊烟就已经开始打磨内部ERP系统，在后台将供应链、厨房、前厅串联起来，进行完备的信息化品控。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>最后，把一个单品做精、做标准，最终做成了自己的品牌。这不仅与如今餐饮界“单品即品牌”的趋势相吻合，也显示出了炊烟对自身菜品的绝对自信。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>谭艳介绍，炊烟小炒黄牛肉全部选用上等黄牛肉，仅选用几个关键部位，炊烟的质检部门会严格把控黄牛肉质量，并且要保证这头牛在宰杀后24小时内上到顾客的桌上。在小炒黄牛肉的炒制技术方面，炊烟也在22年的时间里不断优化制作方法，目前对厨师的要求是30秒内出锅——保证顾客能尝到嫩滑香辣、带有锅气的小炒黄牛肉。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>8月21日，炊烟时代宣布正式更名为炊烟小炒黄牛肉，并推出九大经典湘菜（包括剁椒鱼头、毛氏红烧肉等），以黄兴铜像店为首店开始逐步推广。这家位于长沙最热闹商圈、最吸引游人的黄兴铜像店也将营业至凌晨2点、开发夜宵。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden center break-word><img data-ratio=\"0.6650602409638554\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"830\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box; vertical-align: top; display: inline; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/LrRuh3G4W5znch9tZfChic7micsaiaxeXhCdchR2xlPEKiat51UDBSVQFMp7QfepLZtaFFGp6u8RQdPfucj2wh5D1g/640?wx_fmt=png\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>肖志军认为，目前，湘菜正处于从“量变”到“质变”、从大众消费向品牌消费过度的阶段，炊烟的一路升级恰好能够代表这个趋势。由于炊烟小炒黄牛肉的品牌价值不断增强，其品牌影响力、对整个湘菜产业的带动效应也会越来越强。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p label=\"大标题\" style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden bold center break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;display: block;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;width: 265px !important;\"><em style=\"margin-top: 9px;margin-right: 10px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;width: 12px;display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;background-size: 100% 100%;height: 8px;background-image: url(\" https: no-repeat break-word></em><span style=\"box-sizing: border-box;display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;z-index: 10000;line-height: 1.65;max-width: 250px !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">中国进入牛肉时代</span><em style=\"margin-top: 8px;margin-left: 10px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;width: 12px;display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;background-size: 100% 100%;height: 11px;background-image: url(\" https: no-repeat break-word></em></span></span></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>事实上，炊烟选择的方向与中国肉类饮食消费的变化走向相同。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>牛肉以高蛋白、口感好著称，同猪肉相比，脂肪更低，与鸡肉相比，胆固醇较低，还富含多种微量元素。因此，牛肉在发达国家的肉类消费结构中占重要比重。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>比如酷爱吃牛肉的美国人——美国农业部（USDA）数据显示，2019年美国人均牛肉消费量为57.3磅，约合26.0公斤。而根据中商产业研究院数据，2019年中国人均牛肉消费量约为5.95公斤，仅为美国人均消费量的23%。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>也因此，牛肉消费在中国大有潜力。数据显示，中国的牛肉消费量正在迅速增长：2019年，我国牛肉消费量为832.93万吨，同比增长11.36%，这是近三年来的最大增幅。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>小炒黄牛肉，是炊烟吸引顾客的“关键一招”。但炊烟的目标更为宏大：要重新赋予那些经典湘菜们生机，把它们带给更多的人、推向更大的舞台。它们可能已经不那么“洋气”、不是现在年轻人最常点的菜品，在炊烟对食材、做法进行全面升级后，那些湖南人记忆里的辣与香，必将重新升腾起热气。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>湖南的餐饮商业环境与湖湘文化密不可分。“吃得苦、霸得蛮、耐得烦”的湖南人性格，注定了餐饮湘军的激烈竞争。炊烟凭借一道小炒黄牛肉从一片混沌的湘菜餐饮市场中“杀”出，将品类品牌化、凸显品牌的价值，成为湘菜品质的代表，也成了一张长沙的名片。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word>小炒黄牛肉上桌，热气袅袅升起——是人间烟火气，也是长沙。</p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb hidden break-word><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"padding-right: 8px;padding-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);font-family: \" helvetica neue hidden flex center justify space-between start break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;width: 527.156px;height: 4px;border-radius: 4px;background-color: rgb(255, 128, 128);border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(230, 230, 230);overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 12px;line-height: 1;color: rgb(187, 187, 187);text-align: right;width: 130px;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">特别策划</span></p>\n                </div>\n\n    \n    <br>\n\n    \n        <a target=\"_blank\"
